<TEXT>
Artificial intelligence is changing how people build software.
<END>


<TEXT>
Machine learning helps computers learn patterns from data.
<END>


<TEXT>
Deep learning uses neural networks with many layers.
<END>


<TEXT>
Generative AI can create text, code, summaries, and reports.
<END>


<TEXT>
Transformers use attention to understand relationships in data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A tokenizer converts text into numbers for a machine learning model.
<END>


<TEXT>
A dataset provides examples that a model can learn from.
<END>


<TEXT>
Training is the process of updating model weights using data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A checkpoint stores the learned parameters of a trained model.
<END>


<TEXT>
PyTorch is a deep learning framework used to build neural networks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Artificial intelligence allows machines to perform tasks that normally require human intelligence such as reasoning, learning, and decision making.
Summary: Artificial intelligence enables machines to perform intelligent tasks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Machine learning is a subset of artificial intelligence where systems learn patterns from data instead of being explicitly programmed.
Summary: Machine learning helps systems learn from data.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Generative AI creates new content such as text, images, code, reports, summaries, music, and videos.
Summary: Generative AI creates new content.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Transformers are deep learning architectures that use attention mechanisms to process sequence data effectively.
Summary: Transformers use attention to understand sequences.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: A tokenizer converts raw text into numerical tokens that can be processed by a neural network.
Summary: A tokenizer converts text into numbers.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.
Methodology: A decoder-only Transformer was built from scratch using PyTorch and trained with next-character prediction.
Result: The model learned to generate simple AI-related text.
Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Fraud Detection AI
Problem Statement: Financial institutions need to identify fraudulent transactions quickly.
Methodology: A machine learning model was trained using transaction features and evaluated with precision, recall, and F1-score.
Result: The model detected suspicious transaction patterns.
Conclusion: The system can support financial fraud monitoring.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Medical Report Generator
Problem Statement: Medical professionals need fast and consistent report generation support.
Methodology: A vision-language model was designed to generate reports from medical images.
Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.
Conclusion: Generative AI can assist clinical documentation workflows.
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that adds two numbers.
Code:
def add_numbers(a, b):
    return a + b
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that checks if a number is even.
Code:
def is_even(number):
    return number % 2 == 0
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that calculates the square of a number.
Code:
def square(number):
    return number * number
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a FastAPI health endpoint.
Code:
from fastapi import FastAPI

app = FastAPI()

@app.get("/health")
def health_check():
    return {"status": "ok"}
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is Retrieval-Augmented Generation?
Answer: RAG means Retrieval-Augmented Generation. It retrieves relevant external information before generating an answer.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is MiniGenAI?
Answer: MiniGenAI is a Transformer-based generative AI model built from scratch using PyTorch.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>

<REPORT>
Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.
Methodology: A decoder-only Transformer was built from scratch using PyTorch and trained with next-character prediction.
Result: The model learned to generate simple AI-related text.
Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
<END>

Project Title: Fraud Detection AI
Problem Statement: Financial institutions need to identify fraudulent transactions quickly.
Methodology: A machine learning model was trained using transaction features and evaluated with precision, recall, and F1-score.
Result: The model detected suspicious transaction patterns.
Conclusion: The system can support financial fraud monitoring.
<END>

Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.

Question: What is Retrieval-Augmented Generation?
Answer: RAG means Retrieval-Augmented Generation. It retrieves relevant external information before generating an answer.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is MiniGenAI?
Answer: MiniGenAI is a Transformer-based generative AI model built from scratch using PyTorch.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>

<END>

Problem Statement: Medical professionals need fast and consistent report generation support.
Methodology: A vision-language model was designed to generate reports from medical images.
Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.
Conclusion: Generative AI can assist clinical documentation workflows.
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that adds two numbers.
Code:
def add_numbers(a, b):
    return a + b
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that checks if a number is even.
Code:
def is_even(number):
    return number % 2 == 0
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that calculates the square of a number.
Code:
def square(number):
    return number * number
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a FastAPI health endpoint.
Code:
from fastapi import FastAPI

app = FastAPI()

@app.get("/health")
def health_check():
    return {"status": "ok"}
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is Retrieval-Augmented Generation?
Answer: RAG means Retrieval-Augmented Generation. It retrieves relevant external information before generating an answer.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is MiniGenAI?
Answer: MiniGenAI is a Transformer-based generative AI model built from scratch using PyTorch.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>

app = FastAPI()

@app.get("/health")
def health_check():
    return {"status": "ok"}
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is Retrieval-Augmented Generation?
Answer: RAG means Retrieval-Augmented Generation. It retrieves relevant external information before generating an answer.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is MiniGenAI?
Answer: MiniGenAI is a Transformer-based generative AI model built from scratch using PyTorch.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>


<TEXT>
Artificial intelligence is changing how people build software.
<END>


<TEXT>
Machine learning helps computers learn patterns from data.
<END>


<TEXT>
Deep learning uses neural networks with many layers.
<END>


<TEXT>
Generative AI can create text, code, summaries, and reports.
<END>


<TEXT>
Transformers use attention to understand relationships in data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A tokenizer converts text into numbers for a machine learning model.
<END>


<TEXT>
A dataset provides examples that a model can learn from.
<END>


<TEXT>
Training is the process of updating model weights using data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A checkpoint stores the learned parameters of a trained model.
<END>


<TEXT>
PyTorch is a deep learning framework used to build neural networks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Artificial intelligence allows machines to perform tasks that normally require human intelligence such as reasoning, learning, and decision making.
Summary: Artificial intelligence enables machines to perform intelligent tasks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Machine learning is a subset of artificial intelligence where systems learn patterns from data instead of being explicitly programmed.
Summary: Machine learning helps systems learn from data.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Generative AI creates new content such as text, images, code, reports, summaries, music, and videos.
Summary: Generative AI creates new content.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Transformers are deep learning architectures that use attention mechanisms to process sequence data effectively.
Summary: Transformers use attention to understand sequences.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: A tokenizer converts raw text into numerical tokens that can be processed by a neural network.
Summary: A tokenizer converts text into numbers.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.
Methodology: A decoder-only Transformer was built from scratch using PyTorch and trained with next-character prediction.
Result: The model learned to generate simple AI-related text.
Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Fraud Detection AI
Problem Statement: Financial institutions need to identify fraudulent transactions quickly.
Methodology: A machine learning model was trained using transaction features and evaluated with precision, recall, and F1-score.
Result: The model detected suspicious transaction patterns.
Conclusion: The system can support financial fraud monitoring.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Medical Report Generator
Problem Statement: Medical professionals need fast and consistent report generation support.
Methodology: A vision-language model was designed to generate reports from medical images.
Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.
Conclusion: Generative AI can assist clinical documentation workflows.
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that adds two numbers.
Code:
def add_numbers(a, b):
    return a + b
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that checks if a number is even.
Code:
def is_even(number):
    return number % 2 == 0
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that calculates the square of a number.
Code:
def square(number):
    return number * number
<END>

Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.

Summary: A tokenizer converts text into numbers.

Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.

Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.

Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.

<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.

from fastapi import FastAPI

app = FastAPI()

@app.get("/health")
def health_check():
    return {"status": "ok"}
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is Retrieval-Augmented Generation?
Answer: RAG means Retrieval-Augmented Generation. It retrieves relevant external information before generating an answer.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What is MiniGenAI?
Answer: MiniGenAI is a Transformer-based generative AI model built from scratch using PyTorch.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: What does a checkpoint store?
Answer: A checkpoint stores the trained model weights and tokenizer vocabulary.
<END>


<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?
Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>


<TEXT>
Artificial intelligence is changing how people build software.
<END>


<TEXT>
Machine learning helps computers learn patterns from data.
<END>


<TEXT>
Deep learning uses neural networks with many layers.
<END>


<TEXT>
Generative AI can create text, code, summaries, and reports.
<END>


<TEXT>
Transformers use attention to understand relationships in data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A tokenizer converts text into numbers for a machine learning model.
<END>


<TEXT>
A dataset provides examples that a model can learn from.
<END>


<TEXT>
Training is the process of updating model weights using data.
<END>


<TEXT>
A checkpoint stores the learned parameters of a trained model.
<END>


<TEXT>
PyTorch is a deep learning framework used to build neural networks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Artificial intelligence allows machines to perform tasks that normally require human intelligence such as reasoning, learning, and decision making.
Summary: Artificial intelligence enables machines to perform intelligent tasks.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Machine learning is a subset of artificial intelligence where systems learn patterns from data instead of being explicitly programmed.
Summary: Machine learning helps systems learn from data.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Generative AI creates new content such as text, images, code, reports, summaries, music, and videos.
Summary: Generative AI creates new content.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: Transformers are deep learning architectures that use attention mechanisms to process sequence data effectively.
Summary: Transformers use attention to understand sequences.
<END>


<SUMMARY>
Long Text: A tokenizer converts raw text into numerical tokens that can be processed by a neural network.
Summary: A tokenizer converts text into numbers.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.
Methodology: A decoder-only Transformer was built from scratch using PyTorch and trained with next-character prediction.
Result: The model learned to generate simple AI-related text.
Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Fraud Detection AI
Problem Statement: Financial institutions need to identify fraudulent transactions quickly.
Methodology: A machine learning model was trained using transaction features and evaluated with precision, recall, and F1-score.
Result: The model detected suspicious transaction patterns.
Conclusion: The system can support financial fraud monitoring.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Medical Report Generator
Problem Statement: Medical professionals need fast and consistent report generation support.
Methodology: A vision-language model was designed to generate reports from medical images.
Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.
Conclusion: Generative AI can assist clinical documentation workflows.
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that adds two numbers.
Code:
def add_numbers(a, b):
    return a + b
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that checks if a number is even.
Code:
def is_even(number):
    return number % 2 == 0
<END>


<CODE>
Task: Create a Python function that calculates the square of a number.
Code:
def square(number):
    return number * number
<END>

Answer: Word-level tokenization helps the model learn full words instead of individual letters, which improves output quality.
<END>

<REPORT>
Project Title: MiniGenAI
Problem Statement: Many beginners use AI tools without understanding how generative models work internally.
Methodology: A decoder-only Transformer was built from scratch using PyTorch and trained with next-character prediction.
Result: The model learned to generate simple AI-related text.
Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Fraud Detection AI
Problem Statement: Financial institutions need to identify fraudulent transactions quickly.
Methodology: A machine learning model was trained using transaction features and evaluated with precision, recall, and F1-score.
Result: The model detected suspicious transaction patterns.
Conclusion: The system can support financial fraud monitoring.
<END>


<REPORT>
Project Title: Medical Report Generator
Problem Statement: Medical professionals need fast and consistent report generation support.
Methodology: A vision-language model was designed to generate reports from medical images.
Result: The system produced structured draft medical reports.
Conclusion: Generative AI can assist clinical documentation workflows.
<END>

<ANSWER>
Question: Why is word-level tokenization better than character-level tokenization?

<END>

Long Text: A tokenizer converts raw text into numerical tokens that can be processed by a neural network.
Summary: A tokenizer converts text into numbers.

Project Title: MiniGenAI

Conclusion: MiniGenAI demonstrates the foundation of GPT-style generative AI.
